# 增强对照表（源英文 → 加强英文 → 中文本地化）

> spec 共 48 个接口，1204 个对外字段/参数。逐字段对照「原文 → 加强 → 本地化」三态，判断改得更好还是更坏。

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_dataforseo_trends_merged_data_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with the keyword popularity data from DataForSEO Trends. In addition to keyword popularity rate over the given time range, you will get location-specific keyword popularity data, and a demographic breakdown of keyword popularity per each specified term along with comparative values. | Run a DataForSEO Trends 合并数据 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 DataForSEO Trends 合并数据 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field the maximum number of keywords you can specify: 5 avoid symbols and special characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis); specifying non-Latin characters, you’ll get data for the countries where they are used learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_name belongs to; example: United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_code belongs to; example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.type` | dataforseo trends type optional field if you don’t specify this field, the web type will be used by default possible values: web, news, ecommerce | Trends data category to query (e.g. web, news, ecommerce). Selects which corpus the popularity figures are drawn from. | 要查询的趋势数据类别（如 web、news、ecommerce），决定热度数据取自哪一类语料。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the current day and month of the preceding year will be used by default minimal value for the web type: 2004-01-01 minimal value for other types: 2008-01-01 date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the today’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.time_range` | preset time ranges optional field if you specify date_from or date_to parameters, this field will be ignored when setting a task possible values for all type parameters: past_4_hours, past_day, past_7_days, past_30_days, past_90_days, past_12_months, past_5_years | Preset relative time window for trend data, used as a shortcut instead of date_from/date_to. Ignored if explicit dates are supplied. | 趋势数据的预设相对时间窗，作为 date_from/date_to 的快捷替代；若已显式给定日期则忽略本字段。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keywords` | keywords in a POST array | The keywords submitted in the request that this result corresponds to. | 本结果对应的、请求中提交的关键词列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.type` | search engine type in a POST array | Search-engine/data type echoed from the request. | 从请求回显的搜索引擎/数据类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | UTC timestamp when this result was produced. | 本结果生成的 UTC 时间戳。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of entries in this result's items array. | 本结果 items 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keyword popularity and related data | Detailed per-keyword (or per-element) data rows for this result. | 本结果中按关键词（或按元素）的明细数据行。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.position` | the alignment of the element can take the following values: 1, 2, 3, 4, etc. | Ordinal position of this element within the items array. | 本元素在 items 数组中的序号位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.type` | type of element = ‘demography’ | Element type of this item row, indicating which kind of data block it carries. | 本条目的元素类型，指明它承载的数据块类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keywords` | relevant keywords the data included in the demography and demography_comparison is based on the keywords listed in this array | Keywords that the demography and comparison data in this item are based on. | 本条目中人口统计与对比数据所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data` | DataForSEO Trends data for the specified parameters | Trends time-series data points for the requested parameters. | 针对所请求参数的趋势时间序列数据点。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.date_from` | start date of the corresponding time range in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd” | Start date (UTC) of this data point's time bucket. | 该数据点所属时间桶的起始日期（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.date_to` | end date of the corresponding time range in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd” | End date (UTC) of this data point's time bucket. | 该数据点所属时间桶的结束日期（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.timestamp` | a point in time in the Unix time format | Point in time of this data point, in Unix time. | 该数据点的时间点，Unix 时间格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.values` | relative keyword popularity rate at a specific timestamp if you specify more than one keyword, the values will be averaged to the highest value across all specified keywords a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity at this timestamp; when multiple keywords are queried the values are averaged. The scale is relative, peaking at the most popular point. | 该时间点的相对关键词热度；查询多个关键词时取平均。该刻度为相对值，在最热点处达到峰值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.averages` | keyword popularity values averaged over the whole time range | Keyword popularity values averaged across the full requested time range. | 在整个所请求时间范围内取平均的关键词热度值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests` | subregional keyword popuarity data for each specified term | Subregional keyword popularity data for each specified term. | 每个指定词的次区域关键词热度数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.keyword` | relevant keyword the data included in the values element is based on this keyword | Keyword the subregional values are based on. | 次区域数值所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values` | contains data on relative keyword popularity by country or region | Relative keyword popularity broken down by country or region. | 按国家或地区拆分的相对关键词热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to the location parameters in your request. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求中的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to the location parameters in your request. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求中的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.value` | relative keyword popularity rate in a given location represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is in one location compared to another location; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all locations, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Location-specific relative keyword popularity over the requested time range. | 在所请求时间范围内某位置的相对关键词热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison` | comparison of data on subregional keyword popularity for the specified parameters if you specified a single keyword, the value will be null | Comparison of subregional popularity across the specified terms; null when only one keyword was supplied. | 对所指定多个词的次区域热度对比；仅提交一个关键词时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items` | keyword popularity values per location values in this array represent percentages relative to the maximum value within each region | Per-location popularity values normalized relative to the maximum within each region. | 按位置的热度值，相对每个地区内的最大值做归一化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.values` | keyword popularity rates within a given location represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using these values, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular in the related location; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value across all specified keywords within a given location, and then express the popularity values of each keyword as a percentage of the highest value (100); a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative popularity within the given location over the requested time range. | 在所请求时间范围内某位置内的相对热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items` | keyword popularity rates across all locations values in this array represent percentages relative to the maximum value across all locations | Per-location popularity values normalized relative to the maximum across all locations. | 按位置的热度值，相对所有位置中的最大值做归一化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.values` | keyword popularity rates relative to all locations represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using these values, you can understand how popular each keyword is compared to all other keywords across all locations; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value across all keywords across all locations, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Location-specific relative popularity, normalized across all locations. | 某位置的相对热度，跨所有位置做归一化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography` | demographic breakdown of keyword popularity data per each specified term conains keyword popularity data by age and gender | Demographic breakdown of keyword popularity, split by age and gender for each term. | 关键词热度的人口统计拆分，按年龄与性别分别给出每个词的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age` | distribution of keyword popularity by age | Keyword popularity distributed across age ranges. | 关键词热度在各年龄段上的分布。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.keyword` | relevant keyword for which demographic data is provided | Keyword the age-distribution data applies to. | 年龄分布数据所对应的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values` | contains age range and corresponding keyword popularity values | Age-range buckets with their corresponding popularity values. | 各年龄段及其对应的热度值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values.type` | age range can take the following values: 18-24, 25-34, 35-44, 45-54, 55-64 | The age range this value applies to. | 该热度值所对应的年龄段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values.value` | keyword popularity rate within the specified age range using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is within each age range; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all age groups, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity within this age range, on the trends popularity scale. | 该年龄段内关键词的相对热度，采用趋势热度刻度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender` | distribution of keyword popularity by gender | Keyword popularity distributed across gender categories. | 关键词热度在各性别类别上的分布。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.keyword` | relevant keyword for which demographic data is provided | Keyword the gender-distribution data applies to. | 性别分布数据所对应的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values` | contains gender and corresponding keyword popularity values | Gender categories with their corresponding popularity values. | 各性别类别及其对应的热度值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values.type` | gender category can take the following values: female, male | The gender category this value applies to. | 该热度值所对应的性别类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values.value` | keyword popularity rate within the specified gender category using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is within each gender category; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all gender categories, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term; a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity within this gender category, on the trends popularity scale. | 该性别类别内关键词的相对热度，采用趋势热度刻度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison` | comparison of demographic data on keyword popularity for the specified parameters conains keyword popularity data by age and gender if you specified a single keyword, the value will be null | Side-by-side comparison of demographic popularity across the specified terms; null when only one keyword was supplied. | 对所指定多个词的人口统计热度并排对比；仅提交一个关键词时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.age` | comparison of keyword popularity data by age | Age-based comparison of keyword popularity across terms, keyed by age range. | 按年龄段比较各词关键词热度，以年龄段为键。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.age.$18-24` | indicates age range and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified age range variable can take the following values: 18-24, 18-24, 25-34, 35-44, 45-54, 55-64; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related age range; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each age range, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the corresponding age range across the specified terms. | 对应年龄段下各指定词的对比数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender` | comparison of keyword popularity data by gender | Gender-based comparison of keyword popularity across terms, keyed by gender category. | 按性别类别比较各词关键词热度，以性别类别为键。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender.female` | indicates gender category and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified gender category; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related gender category; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each gender category, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the female category across the specified terms. | female 类别下各指定词的对比数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender.male` | indicates gender category and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified gender category; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related gender category; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each gender category, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the male category across the specified terms. | male 类别下各指定词的对比数值。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_audience_estimation_industries

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Pricing | Return the reference list of Bing 广告受众估算 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 Bing 广告受众估算 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the URL of the GET request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.industry_id` | ID of the industry | Identifier of the LinkedIn industry. | LinkedIn 行业的标识。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.industry_name` | name of the industry | Name of the LinkedIn industry. | LinkedIn 行业的名称。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_audience_estimation_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides estimated audience size for an ad campaign based on specified targeting criteria. It returns data on the total estimated audience, such as suggested bid and budget for an ad campaign and estimated engagement metrics. | Run a Bing 广告受众估算 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing 广告受众估算 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude,radius (in km)” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 29.6821525,-82.4098881,100 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.age` | selection of age ranges for targeting possible values: eighteen_to_twenty_four, fifty_to_sixty_four, sixty_five_and_above, thirteen_to_seventeen, thirty_five_to_forty_nine, twenty_five_to_thirty_four, unknown, zero_to_twelve | Age-range buckets to target for the audience estimate, passed as an array. Narrows the estimated audience to the chosen demographics. | 受众估算的目标年龄段，以数组传入，用于把估算受众收窄到所选人群。 |
| `req.bid` | desired bid setting value in USD maximum value: 1000 | Hypothetical max bid in USD used to forecast ad traffic. Drives the estimated impressions, clicks, and spend figures returned. | 用于预测广告流量的假设最高出价（美元），决定返回的预计展示、点击与花费数据。 |
| `req.daily_budget` | daily campaign budget value in USD maximum value: 10000 | Hypothetical daily campaign budget in USD used to forecast ad traffic, constraining the estimated reach and spend. | 用于预测广告流量的假设每日预算（美元），会约束返回的预计触达与花费。 |
| `req.gender` | gender to target possible values: male, female, unknown | Gender categories to target for the audience estimate, passed as an array. Narrows the estimated audience to the chosen demographics. | 受众估算的目标性别类别，以数组传入，用于把估算受众收窄到所选人群。 |
| `req.industry` | industry of LinkedIn profile targeting if you use this field, you can receive the list of available industry names with industry_id by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/audience_estimation/industries example: 806301758 | LinkedIn industry IDs to target for the audience estimate. Resolve valid IDs and names via the audience_estimation/industries endpoint. | 受众估算的目标 LinkedIn 行业 ID。可通过 audience_estimation/industries 端点查询合法 ID 与名称。 |
| `req.job_function` | job function of LinkedIn profile targeting if you use this field, you can receive the list of available job function names with job_function_id by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/audience_estimation/job_functions example: 806300451 | LinkedIn job-function IDs to target for the audience estimate. Resolve valid IDs and names via the audience_estimation/job_functions endpoint. | 受众估算的目标 LinkedIn 职能 ID。可通过 audience_estimation/job_functions 端点查询合法 ID 与名称。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_audience_estimation_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides estimated audience size for an ad campaign based on specified targeting criteria. It returns data on the total estimated audience, such as suggested bid and budget for an ad campaign and estimated engagement metrics. | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing 广告受众估算 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing 广告受众估算 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_audience_estimation_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides estimated audience size for an ad campaign based on specified targeting criteria. It returns data on the total estimated audience, such as suggested bid and budget for an ad campaign and estimated engagement metrics. | Queue a Bing 广告受众估算 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Bing 广告受众估算 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude,radius (in km)” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 29.6821525,-82.4098881,100 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.age` | selection of age ranges for targeting possible values: eighteen_to_twenty_four, fifty_to_sixty_four, sixty_five_and_above, thirteen_to_seventeen, thirty_five_to_forty_nine, twenty_five_to_thirty_four, unknown, zero_to_twelve | Age-range buckets to target for the audience estimate, passed as an array. Narrows the estimated audience to the chosen demographics. | 受众估算的目标年龄段，以数组传入，用于把估算受众收窄到所选人群。 |
| `req.bid` | desired bid setting value in USD maximum value: 1000 | Hypothetical max bid in USD used to forecast ad traffic. Drives the estimated impressions, clicks, and spend figures returned. | 用于预测广告流量的假设最高出价（美元），决定返回的预计展示、点击与花费数据。 |
| `req.daily_budget` | daily campaign budget value in USD maximum value: 10000 | Hypothetical daily campaign budget in USD used to forecast ad traffic, constraining the estimated reach and spend. | 用于预测广告流量的假设每日预算（美元），会约束返回的预计触达与花费。 |
| `req.gender` | gender to target possible values: male, female, unknown | Gender categories to target for the audience estimate, passed as an array. Narrows the estimated audience to the chosen demographics. | 受众估算的目标性别类别，以数组传入，用于把估算受众收窄到所选人群。 |
| `req.industry` | industry of LinkedIn profile targeting if you use this field, you can receive the list of available industry names with industry_id by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/audience_estimation/industries example: 806301758 | LinkedIn industry IDs to target for the audience estimate. Resolve valid IDs and names via the audience_estimation/industries endpoint. | 受众估算的目标 LinkedIn 行业 ID。可通过 audience_estimation/industries 端点查询合法 ID 与名称。 |
| `req.job_function` | job function of LinkedIn profile targeting if you use this field, you can receive the list of available job function names with job_function_id by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/audience_estimation/job_functions example: 806300451 | LinkedIn job-function IDs to target for the audience estimate. Resolve valid IDs and names via the audience_estimation/job_functions endpoint. | 受众估算的目标 LinkedIn 职能 ID。可通过 audience_estimation/job_functions 端点查询合法 ID 与名称。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | unique task identifier in our system unique task identifier in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_performance_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | You can receive a set of keyword performance stats for a group of keywords depending on the specified match type, location and language parameters. Ad position, clicks, impressions, and other keyword metrics are aggregated for the last month for one or all of the following device types: mobile, desktop, tablet. | Run a Bing 关键词效果 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing 关键词效果 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 The maximum number of words for each keyword phrase: 10 the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device typepossible values: desktop, mobile, tablet, all default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.match` | keywords match type optional field can take the following values: aggregate returns data across all match types; broad returns data for all user queries containing the specified keyword with varying word order; phrase returns data for all user queries containing the specified keyword with identical word order; exact returns data for user query that matches the specified keyword;Note: the aggregate match type is applied by default | Keyword match type that controls how strictly user queries must match your keyword (aggregate / broad / phrase / exact), shaping which queries contribute to the metrics. | 关键词匹配类型，控制用户查询需与关键词匹配的严格程度（aggregate / broad / phrase / exact），影响哪些查询计入指标。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: "United States" | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: "en" | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.ad_position` | represents the position of the relevant ad in SERP can take the following values: FirstPage1: The first ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage2: The second ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage3: The third ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage4: The fourth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage5: The fifth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage6: The sixth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage7: The seventh ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage8: The eighth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage9: The ninth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage10: The tenth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page MainLine1: The first ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine2: The second ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine3: The third ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine4: The fourth ad to appear at the top of the search results page | Position of the relevant ad in the SERP for this device. | 该设备上相关广告在 SERP 中的位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.clicks` | ad clicks the number of clicks that the keyword and match type generated during the last month | Ad clicks the keyword and match type generated last month on this device. | 上月该设备上由该关键词与匹配类型带来的广告点击数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.impressions` | ad impressions the number of impressions that the keyword and match type generated during the last month | Ad impressions the keyword and match type generated last month on this device. | 上月该设备上由该关键词与匹配类型带来的广告展示数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.average_cpc` | average cost per click, USD calculated by dividing the cost of all clicks by the number of clicks | Average cost-per-click (USD) on this device, i.e. total cost divided by clicks. | 该设备上的平均每次点击成本（美元），即总花费除以点击数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.ctr` | click-through rate as a percentage calculated by dividing the number of clicks by the number of impressions and multiplying the result by 100 | Click-through rate (%) on this device, i.e. clicks divided by impressions. | 该设备上的点击率（%），即点击数除以展示数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.total_cost` | total cost of an ad, USD the cost of using the specified keyword and match type during the last month | Total ad cost (USD) for the keyword and match type last month on this device. | 上月该设备上该关键词与匹配类型的广告总花费（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.desktop.average_bid` | average bid of the keyword | Average bid for the keyword on this device. | 该设备上该关键词的平均出价。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile` | keyword data aggregated for mobile devices if there is no data, then the value is null | Keyword ad metrics aggregated for mobile devices; null when no data is available. | 按 mobile 设备汇总的关键词广告指标；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.ad_position` | represents the position of the relevant ad in SERP can take the following values: FirstPage1: The first ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage2: The second ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage3: The third ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage4: The fourth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage5: The fifth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage6: The sixth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage7: The seventh ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage8: The eighth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage9: The ninth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage10: The tenth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page MainLine1: The first ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine2: The second ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine3: The third ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine4: The fourth ad to appear at the top of the search results page | Position of the relevant ad in the SERP for this device. | 该设备上相关广告在 SERP 中的位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.clicks` | ad clicks the number of clicks that the keyword and match type generated during the last month | Ad clicks the keyword and match type generated last month on this device. | 上月该设备上由该关键词与匹配类型带来的广告点击数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.impressions` | ad impressions the number of impressions that the keyword and match type generated during the last month | Ad impressions the keyword and match type generated last month on this device. | 上月该设备上由该关键词与匹配类型带来的广告展示数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.average_cpc` | average cost per click, USD calculated by dividing the cost of all clicks by the number of clicks | Average cost-per-click (USD) on this device, i.e. total cost divided by clicks. | 该设备上的平均每次点击成本（美元），即总花费除以点击数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.ctr` | click-through rate as a percentage calculated by dividing the number of clicks by the number of impressions and multiplying the result by 100 | Click-through rate (%) on this device, i.e. clicks divided by impressions. | 该设备上的点击率（%），即点击数除以展示数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.total_cost` | total cost of an ad, USD the cost of using the specified keyword and match type during the last month | Total ad cost (USD) for the keyword and match type last month on this device. | 上月该设备上该关键词与匹配类型的广告总花费（美元）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.mobile.average_bid` | average bid of the keyword | Average bid for the keyword on this device. | 该设备上该关键词的平均出价。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.tablet` | keyword data aggregated for tablet devices if there is no data, then the value is null | Keyword ad metrics aggregated for tablet devices; null when no data is available. | 按 tablet 设备汇总的关键词广告指标；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_kpi.tablet.ad_position` | represents the position of the relevant ad in SERP can take the following values: FirstPage1: The first ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage2: The second ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage3: The third ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage4: The fourth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage5: The fifth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage6: The sixth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage7: The seventh ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage8: The eighth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage9: The ninth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page FirstPage10: The tenth ad to appear on the right side of the first search results page MainLine1: The first ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine2: The second ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine3: The third ad to appear at the top of the search results page MainLine4: The fourth ad to appear at the top of the search results page | Position of the relevant ad in the SERP for this device. | 该设备上相关广告在 SERP 中的位置。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_performance_locations_and_languages

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Using this endpoint you can get the full list of locations and languages supported in Keyword Performance endpoints of Bing Keywords Data API. | Return the reference list of Bing 关键词效果 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 Bing 关键词效果 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the URL of the GET request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_name` | language name | Language name for the returned data. | 返回数据对应的语言名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_locations` | supported locations contains locations supported in combination with a specific language | Locations supported in combination with a given language. | 可与给定语言组合使用的受支持位置列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_locations.location_code` | location code | Code of the supported location. | 受支持位置的编码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_locations.location_name` | location name | Name of the supported location. | 受支持位置的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_locations.country_iso_code` | ISO country code of the location | ISO country code of the supported location. | 受支持位置的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_locations.location_type` | location type possible values: Country, Region | Granularity of the supported location, such as country or region. | 受支持位置的粒度，例如国家或地区。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_performance_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | You can receive a set of keyword performance stats for a group of keywords depending on the specified match type, location and language parameters. Ad position, clicks, impressions, and other keyword metrics are aggregated for the last month for one or all of the following device types: mobile, desktop, tablet. | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing 关键词效果 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing 关键词效果 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_performance_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | You can receive a set of keyword performance stats for a group of keywords depending on the specified match type, location and language parameters. Ad position, clicks, impressions, and other keyword metrics are aggregated for the last month for one or all of the following device types: mobile, desktop, tablet. | Queue a Bing 关键词效果 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Bing 关键词效果 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 The maximum number of words for each keyword phrase: 10 the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device typepossible values: desktop, mobile, tablet, all default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.match` | keywords match type optional field can take the following values: aggregate returns data across all match types; broad returns data for all user queries containing the specified keyword with varying word order; phrase returns data for all user queries containing the specified keyword with identical word order; exact returns data for user query that matches the specified keyword;Note: the aggregate match type is applied by default | Keyword match type that controls how strictly user queries must match your keyword (aggregate / broad / phrase / exact), shaping which queries contribute to the metrics. | 关键词匹配类型，控制用户查询需与关键词匹配的严格程度（aggregate / broad / phrase / exact），影响哪些查询计入指标。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: "United States" | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available locations and languages by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_performance/locations_and_languages example: "en" | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | unique task identifier in our system in the Universally unique identifier (UUID) format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_suggestions_for_url_languages

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Pricing | Return the reference list of Bing URL 关键词建议 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 Bing URL 关键词建议 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the URL of the GET request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_name` | language name | Language name for the returned data. | 返回数据对应的语言名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code according to ISO 639-1 | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keyword_suggestions_for_url_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
