| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides keyword suggestions based on the content of a given webpage URL. It analyzes the page and returns a list of relevant keywords, along with a confidence score that indicates the probability that the keyword would match a user’s search query. | Run a Bing URL 关键词建议 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing URL 关键词建议 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.target` | target URL of the webpage to scan for possible keywords required field maximum length: 2000 characters | Target web page (or site) URL to scan for keyword ideas. Combine with target_type to choose page-level or site-level extraction. | 用于抓取关键词建议的目标网页（或站点）URL。与 target_type 搭配，决定按单页还是整站提取。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/keyword_suggestions_for_url/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.exclude_brands` | determines whether the results exclude brand keywords optional field | Whether branded keywords are filtered out of the results. Enable to focus on non-brand demand. | 是否从结果中过滤掉品牌词。开启可聚焦非品牌需求。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array that were returned an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results results are sorted in order from keywords with the highest confidence score to those with the lowest confidence score | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword` | suggested keyword | The keyword these metrics describe (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本组指标所对应的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.confidence_score` | a score from 0.0 to 1.0 that indicates the probability that the keyword would match a user’s search query | Probability (0.0–1.0) that the keyword matches a user's search query; higher means a closer match. | 关键词与用户查询匹配的概率（0.0–1.0），越高表示匹配越紧密。 |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides keyword suggestions based on the content of a given webpage URL. It analyzes the page and returns a list of relevant keywords, along with a confidence score that indicates the probability that the keyword would match a user’s search query. | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing URL 关键词建议 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing URL 关键词建议 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_keywords_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will select the relevant keywords for the specified ones. Set up to 200 keywords and get the results, which are suggested by Bing Ads for your query. You can get up to 3000 keyword suggestions using this function. | Run a Bing 关键词扩展 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing 关键词扩展 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field you can specify the maximum of 200 keywords with each keyword containing no more than 100 characters; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.keywords_negative` | keywords negative array optional field These keywords will be ignored in the results array; You can specify a maximum of 200 terms that you want to exclude from the results; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase format | Negative keyword terms to exclude from the result set. Matching items are dropped from the response and the terms are lowercased before filtering. | 用于从结果中排除的否定关键词。命中的条目会从响应里剔除，过滤前这些词会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device type; possible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field minimal value: 24 months from today’s date; if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword` | keyword in a POST array | The keyword these metrics describe (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本组指标所对应的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_partners` | indicates whether data from partner networks is included in the response | Whether partner-network data was included in this result. | 本结果是否纳入了合作网络的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.device` | device type indicates for what device type the data is provided; possible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet | Device type the data applies to. | 数据所对应的设备类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only. This value is based on Bing Ads data. Possible values: 0.1, 0.5,0.90.1 – low competition, 0.5 – medium competition, 0.9 – high competition; if there is no data the value is null | Relative paid-search competition level for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词在付费搜索中的相对竞争程度；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword. if there is no data, then the value is null | Average historical cost-per-click in USD for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词的历史平均每次点击成本（美元）；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the keyword on the Bing search engine, depending on the user’s targetingsearch volume is rounded to the closest decimal values if there is no data, then the value is null | Approximate monthly average number of searches for the keyword under the requested targeting. | 在所请求定向下，该关键词的月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.categories` | product and service categories legacy field, the value will always be null | Product/service categories for the keyword. Legacy field that is always null. | 关键词的产品/服务类目。该字段为历史遗留，恒为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations. if there is no data, then the value is null | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword over the trailing window. | 该关键词在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate search volume is rounded to the closest decimal values | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_keywords_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will select relevant keywords for the specified terms. Set up to 200 keywords and get the results, which are suggested by Bing Ads for your query. You can get up to 3000 keyword suggestions using this function. | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing 关键词扩展 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing 关键词扩展 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_keywords_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will select relevant keywords for the specified terms. Set up to 200 keywords and get the results, which are suggested by Bing Ads for your query. You can get up to 3000 keyword suggestions using this function. | Queue a Bing 关键词扩展 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Bing 关键词扩展 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field you can specify the maximum of 200 keywords with each keyword containing no more than 100 characters; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.keywords_negative` | keywords negative array optional field These keywords will be ignored in the results array; You can specify a maximum of 200 terms that you want to exclude from the results; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase format | Negative keyword terms to exclude from the result set. Matching items are dropped from the response and the terms are lowercased before filtering. | 用于从结果中排除的否定关键词。命中的条目会从响应里剔除，过滤前这些词会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device type; possible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field minimal value: 24 months from today’s date; if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_site_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords relevant to the specified URL along with their search volume for the last month, search volume trend for up to 24 past months (for estimating search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition values for paid search. The maximum number of returned keywords is **3000.** | Run a Bing 站点关键词 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing 站点关键词 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.target` | domain or URL required field the domain name or URL of the target website | Target web page (or site) URL to scan for keyword ideas. Combine with target_type to choose page-level or site-level extraction. | 用于抓取关键词建议的目标网页（或站点）URL。与 target_type 搭配，决定按单页还是整站提取。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.keywords_negative` | keywords negative array optional field These keywords will be ignored in the results array; You can specify a maximum of 200 terms that you want to exclude from the results; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase format | Negative keyword terms to exclude from the result set. Matching items are dropped from the response and the terms are lowercased before filtering. | 用于从结果中排除的否定关键词。命中的条目会从响应里剔除，过滤前这些词会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device typepossible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field minimal value: 24 months from today’s date; if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array that were returned an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword` | keyword in a POST array | The keyword these metrics describe (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本组指标所对应的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_partners` | indicates whether data from partner networks included in the response | Whether partner-network data was included in this result. | 本结果是否纳入了合作网络的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.device` | device type in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Device type the data applies to. | 数据所对应的设备类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only. This value is based on Bing Ads data. Possible values: 0.1, 0.5,0.90.1 – low competition, 0.5 – medium competition, 0.9 – high competition; if there is no data the value is null | Relative paid-search competition level for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词在付费搜索中的相对竞争程度；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword. if there is no data, then the value is null | Average historical cost-per-click in USD for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词的历史平均每次点击成本（美元）；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the keyword on the Bing search engine, depending on the user’s targetingsearch volume is rounded to the closest decimal valuesif there is no data, then the value is null | Approximate monthly average number of searches for the keyword under the requested targeting. | 在所请求定向下，该关键词的月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.categories` | product and service categories legacy field, the value will always be null | Product/service categories for the keyword. Legacy field that is always null. | 关键词的产品/服务类目。该字段为历史遗留，恒为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations. if there is no data, then the value is null | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword over the trailing window. | 该关键词在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate search volume is rounded to the closest decimal values | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_site_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords relevant to the specified website along with their search volume for the last month, search volume trend for the last year (for estimating search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition level for paid search. The maximum number of returned keywords is **3000.** | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing 站点关键词 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing 站点关键词 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_keywords_for_site_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords relevant to the specified website along with their search volume for the last month, search volume trend for up to 24 past months (for estimating search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition level for paid search. The maximum number of returned keywords is **3000.** | Queue a Bing 站点关键词 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Bing 站点关键词 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.target` | domain or URL required field the URL of the webpage or the domain to scan for possible keywords | Target web page (or site) URL to scan for keyword ideas. Combine with target_type to choose page-level or site-level extraction. | 用于抓取关键词建议的目标网页（或站点）URL。与 target_type 搭配，决定按单页还是整站提取。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.keywords_negative` | keywords negative array optional field These keywords will be ignored in the results array; You can specify a maximum of 200 terms that you want to exclude from the results; the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase format | Negative keyword terms to exclude from the result set. Matching items are dropped from the response and the terms are lowercased before filtering. | 用于从结果中排除的否定关键词。命中的条目会从响应里剔除，过滤前这些词会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device type possible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field minimal value: 24 months from today’s date; if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with search volume data for the last month, search volume trend for up to 24 past months (that will let you estimate search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition values for paid search. | Run a Bing 搜索量 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Bing 搜索量 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 100 the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device type; possible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field minimal value: 24 months from today’s date if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months minimum value: two years back from today’s date date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.device` | device type in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Device type the data applies to. | 数据所对应的设备类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only. This value is based on Bing Ads data. Possible values: 0.1, 0.5,0.90.1 – low competition, 0.5 – medium competition, 0.9 – high competition; if there is no data the value is null | Relative paid-search competition level for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词在付费搜索中的相对竞争程度；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword. if there is no data then the value is null | Average historical cost-per-click in USD for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词的历史平均每次点击成本（美元）；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate represents either the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea on bing search engine depending on the user’s targeting; search volume is rounded to the nearest tens; if there is no data, the value is null | Approximate monthly average number of searches for the keyword under the requested targeting. | 在所请求定向下，该关键词的月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.categories` | product and service categories our API doesn’t return categories for this endpoint: the parameter will always equal null | Product/service categories for the keyword. Legacy field that is always null. | 关键词的产品/服务类目。该字段为历史遗留，恒为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations if there is no data then the value is null | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword over the trailing window. | 该关键词在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate search volume is rounded to the nearest tens | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_search_volume_task_get_id
