| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with search volume data for the last month, search volume trend for the last year (that will let you estimate search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition values for paid search. | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Bing 搜索量 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Bing 搜索量 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_bing_search_volume_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with search volume data for the last month, search volume trend for up to 24 past months (that will let you estimate search volume dynamics), current cost-per-click and competition values for paid search. | Queue a Bing 搜索量 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Bing 搜索量 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 100 the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase, data will be provided in a separate array learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_coordinate if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/bing/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location required field if you don’t specify location_name or location_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if you don’t specify language_code if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code supported languages: English, French, German | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if you don’t specify language_name if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name supported languages: en, fr, de | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.device` | device type optional field specify this field if you want to get the data for a particular device typepossible values: all, mobile, desktop, tablet default value: all | Restricts the returned metrics to a single device type. Leave unset to aggregate across all devices. | 将返回的指标限定到某一设备类型；不设置则跨所有设备汇总。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by search_volume, cpc, competition or relevance in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months minimal value: 24 months from today’s date date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-01-01" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, data will be provided for the last 12 months; minimum value: two years back from today’s date; maximum value: one month from today’s date; note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates; date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2020-03-15" Note: we do not recommend using a custom time range for the past year’s dates | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.search_partners` | Bing search partners type optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Bing, Yahoo, AOL and partner sites that host Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search. default value: false – results are returned for Bing, AOL, and Yahoo search networks | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | unique task identifier in our system unique task identifier in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_clickstream_data_bulk_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | The Bulk Clickstream Search Volume endpoint of DataForSEO Keywords Data API is designed to provide clickstream-based search volume data for up to 1000 keywords in a single Live request. What’s more, it offers historical search volume values for up to 12 months (depending on keywords, location, and language parameters). | Run a 点击流批量搜索量 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 点击流批量搜索量 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | target keywords required field UTF-8 encoding maximum number of keywords you can specify in this array: 1000; each keyword should be at least 3 characters long; the keywords will be converted to lowercase format; Note: certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis) are not allowed to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |

| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of entries in this result's items array. | 本结果 items 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keywords and related data | Detailed per-keyword (or per-element) data rows for this result. | 本结果中按关键词（或按元素）的明细数据行。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | keyword keyword is returned with decoded %## (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) | The keyword this item row describes (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本条目所描述的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_volume` | clickstream-based average monthly search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea based on clickstream you can learn more about clickstream search volume in this Help Center article | Clickstream-based approximate monthly average search volume for the keyword idea. | 基于点击流的关键词创意月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword idea over the trailing window. | 该关键词创意在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_clickstream_data_dataforseo_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with search volume normalized with Bing search volume data or clickstream data for up to 1000 keywords in a single request. | Run a DataForSEO 点击流搜索量 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 DataForSEO 点击流搜索量 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | target keywords required field UTF-8 encoding maximum number of keywords you can specify in this array: 1000 the keywords will be converted to lowercase format Note: certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis) are not allowed to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location required field if you don’t specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code required field if you don’t specify location_name if you use this field, you can receive the list of available locations with location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: 2826 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language required field if don’t specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code required field if don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/clickstream_data/locations_and_languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.use_clickstream` | use clickstream data to provide results optional field if set to true, you will get DataForSEO search volume values based on clickstream data; if set to false, Bing search volume data will be used to calculate DataForSEO search volume; default value: true; Note: Bing search volume is available for locations provided in Bing Search Volume History Locations and Bing Ads Locations endpoints; search volume values for any other location are calculated based on clickstream data even if you set this parameter to false | Whether search-volume values are derived from clickstream data rather than the engine's own figures. Affects which volume methodology is reported. | 搜索量是否基于点击流数据而非引擎自身数据计算，决定返回的搜索量采用哪种口径。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |

| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | ithe number of results returned in the items array | Number of entries in this result's items array. | 本结果 items 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | array of keywords contains keywords and their search volume rates | Detailed per-keyword (or per-element) data rows for this result. | 本结果中按关键词（或按元素）的明细数据行。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | keyword provided in the POST array | The keyword this item row describes (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本条目所描述的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.use_clickstream` | indicates if the use_clickstream parameter is active possible values: true, false | Whether the clickstream option was active when this item was computed. | 计算本条目时是否启用了点击流选项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_volume` | current search volume rate of a keyword | Clickstream-based approximate monthly average search volume for the keyword idea. | 基于点击流的关键词创意月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches` | monthly search volume rates array of objects with search volume rates in a certain month of a year | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword idea over the trailing window. | 该关键词创意在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.monthly_searches.search_volume` | search volume rate in a certain month of a year | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

| `(operation)` | The Clickstream Global Search Volume endpoint of DataForSEO Keywords Data API is designed to provide clickstream-based search volume data for up to 1000 keywords in a single Live request. What’s more, it offers geographical distribution of clickstream search volume values across all available locations. | Run a 点击流全球搜索量 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 点击流全球搜索量 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |

Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.country_distribution` | distribution of clickstream by countries represents clickstream-based search volume in available countries, as well as its respective percentage of global search volume | Breakdown of clickstream search volume by country, with each country's share of global volume. | 点击流搜索量按国家的分布，含各国占全球搜索量的比例。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.country_distribution.country_iso_code` | country ISO code | ISO country code of the distribution entry. | 分布条目所属国家的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.country_distribution.search_volume` | search volume in a given country | Search volume within this country. | 该国内的搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.country_distribution.percentage` | percentage of global search volume | This country's share of global search volume. | 该国占全球搜索量的比例。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_clickstream_data_locations_and_languages

| `(operation)` | Using this endpoint you can get the full list of locations and languages supported in DataForSEO Clickstream Data API. | Return the reference list of 点击流位置与语言 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 点击流位置与语言 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |

| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the parameters passed in the URL of the GET request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_name` | full name of the location | Full name of the location these metrics apply to. | 本组指标所适用位置的全名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code_parent` | the code of the superordinate location the value will be null as Country is the only supported location_type for this API | Location code of the parent (superordinate) location in the geo hierarchy. | 地理层级中上级（父级）位置的位置编码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.country_iso_code` | ISO country code of the location | ISO country code of the location. | 位置所属国家的 ISO 国家代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_type` | location type possible values: Country | Granularity of the location, such as country or region. | 位置的粒度，例如国家或地区。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_languages` | supported languages contains the languages which are supported for a specific location | Languages supported for the given location. | 给定位置所支持的语言列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_languages.language_name` | language name | Name of a supported language. | 受支持语言的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.available_languages.language_code` | language code according to ISO 639-1 | ISO 639-1 code of a supported language. | 受支持语言的 ISO 639-1 代码。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_dataforseo_trends_demography_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with the demographic breakdown (by age and gender) of keyword popularity per each specified term based on DataForSEO Trends data. You can check keyword trends for Google Search, Google News, and Google Shopping. | Run a DataForSEO Trends 人口统计 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 DataForSEO Trends 人口统计 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field the maximum number of keywords you can specify: 5 avoid symbols and special characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis); specifying non-Latin characters, you’ll get data for the countries where they are used learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_name belongs to; example: United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_code belongs to; example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.type` | dataforseo trends type optional field if you don’t specify this field, the web type will be used by default possible values: web, news, ecommerce | Trends data category to query (e.g. web, news, ecommerce). Selects which corpus the popularity figures are drawn from. | 要查询的趋势数据类别（如 web、news、ecommerce），决定热度数据取自哪一类语料。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the current day and month of the preceding year will be used by default minimal value for the web type: 2004-01-01 minimal value for other types: 2008-01-01 date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the today’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.time_range` | preset time ranges optional field if you specify date_from or date_to parameters, this field will be ignored when setting a task possible values for all type parameters: past_4_hours, past_day, past_7_days, past_30_days, past_90_days, past_12_months, past_5_years | Preset relative time window for trend data, used as a shortcut instead of date_from/date_to. Ignored if explicit dates are supplied. | 趋势数据的预设相对时间窗，作为 date_from/date_to 的快捷替代；若已显式给定日期则忽略本字段。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keywords` | keywords in a POST array | The keywords submitted in the request that this result corresponds to. | 本结果对应的、请求中提交的关键词列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.type` | search engine type in a POST array | Search-engine/data type echoed from the request. | 从请求回显的搜索引擎/数据类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | UTC timestamp when this result was produced. | 本结果生成的 UTC 时间戳。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of entries in this result's items array. | 本结果 items 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keyword popularity and related data | Detailed per-keyword (or per-element) data rows for this result. | 本结果中按关键词（或按元素）的明细数据行。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.position` | the alignment of the element can take the following values: 1, 2, 3, 4, etc. | Ordinal position of this element within the items array. | 本元素在 items 数组中的序号位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.type` | type of element = ‘demography’ | Element type of this item row, indicating which kind of data block it carries. | 本条目的元素类型，指明它承载的数据块类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keywords` | relevant keywords the data included in the demography and demography_comparison is based on the keywords listed in this array | Keywords that the demography and comparison data in this item are based on. | 本条目中人口统计与对比数据所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography` | demographic breakdown of keyword popularity data per each specified term conains keyword popularity data by age and gender | Demographic breakdown of keyword popularity, split by age and gender for each term. | 关键词热度的人口统计拆分，按年龄与性别分别给出每个词的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age` | distribution of keyword popularity by age | Keyword popularity distributed across age ranges. | 关键词热度在各年龄段上的分布。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.keyword` | relevant keyword for which demographic data is provided | Keyword the age-distribution data applies to. | 年龄分布数据所对应的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values` | contains age range and corresponding keyword popularity values | Age-range buckets with their corresponding popularity values. | 各年龄段及其对应的热度值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values.type` | age range can take the following values: 18-24, 25-34, 35-44, 45-54, 55-64 | The age range this value applies to. | 该热度值所对应的年龄段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.age.values.value` | keyword popularity rate within the specified age range using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is within each age range; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all age groups, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity within this age range, on the trends popularity scale. | 该年龄段内关键词的相对热度，采用趋势热度刻度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender` | distribution of keyword popularity by gender | Keyword popularity distributed across gender categories. | 关键词热度在各性别类别上的分布。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.keyword` | relevant keyword for which demographic data is provided | Keyword the gender-distribution data applies to. | 性别分布数据所对应的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values` | contains gender and corresponding keyword popularity values | Gender categories with their corresponding popularity values. | 各性别类别及其对应的热度值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values.type` | gender category can take the following values: female, male | The gender category this value applies to. | 该热度值所对应的性别类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography.gender.values.value` | keyword popularity rate within the specified gender category using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is within each gender category; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all gender categories, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term; a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity within this gender category, on the trends popularity scale. | 该性别类别内关键词的相对热度，采用趋势热度刻度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison` | comparison of demographic data on keyword popularity for the specified parameters conains keyword popularity data by age and gender if you specified a single keyword, the value will be null | Side-by-side comparison of demographic popularity across the specified terms; null when only one keyword was supplied. | 对所指定多个词的人口统计热度并排对比；仅提交一个关键词时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.age` | comparison of keyword popularity data by age | Age-based comparison of keyword popularity across terms, keyed by age range. | 按年龄段比较各词关键词热度，以年龄段为键。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.age.$18-24` | indicates age range and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified age range variable can take the following values: 18-24, 25-34, 35-44, 45-54, 55-64; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related age range; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each age range, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the corresponding age range across the specified terms. | 对应年龄段下各指定词的对比数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender` | comparison of keyword popularity data by gender | Gender-based comparison of keyword popularity across terms, keyed by gender category. | 按性别类别比较各词关键词热度，以性别类别为键。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender.female` | indicates gender category and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified gender category; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related gender category; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each gender category, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the female category across the specified terms. | female 类别下各指定词的对比数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.demography_comparison.gender.male` | indicates gender category and contains corresponding keyword popularity values contains comparison of keyword popularity for the specified terms within the specified gender category; using the values from this array, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular within the related gender category; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the total popularity value of all keywords within each gender category, and then express all other values as a percentage of the total value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Comparison values for the male category across the specified terms. | male 类别下各指定词的对比数值。 |

| `req.time_range` | preset time ranges optional field if you specify date_from or date_to parameters, this field will be ignored when setting a task possible values for all type parameters: past_4_hours, past_day, past_7_days, past_30_days, past_90_days, past_12_months, past_5_years | Preset relative time window for trend data, used as a shortcut instead of date_from/date_to. Ignored if explicit dates are supplied. | 趋势数据的预设相对时间窗，作为 date_from/date_to 的快捷替代；若已显式给定日期则忽略本字段。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keywords` | keywords in a POST array | The keywords submitted in the request that this result corresponds to. | 本结果对应的、请求中提交的关键词列表。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.type` | search engine type in a POST array | Search-engine/data type echoed from the request. | 从请求回显的搜索引擎/数据类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.datetime` | date and time when the result was received in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | UTC timestamp when this result was produced. | 本结果生成的 UTC 时间戳。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of entries in this result's items array. | 本结果 items 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keyword popularity and related data | Detailed per-keyword (or per-element) data rows for this result. | 本结果中按关键词（或按元素）的明细数据行。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.position` | the alignment of the element can take the following values: 1, 2, 3, 4, etc. | Ordinal position of this element within the items array. | 本元素在 items 数组中的序号位置。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.type` | type of element = ‘dataforseo_trends_graph’ | Element type of this item row, indicating which kind of data block it carries. | 本条目的元素类型，指明它承载的数据块类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keywords` | relevant keywords the data included in the dataforseo_trends_graph element is based on the keywords listed in this array | Keywords that the demography and comparison data in this item are based on. | 本条目中人口统计与对比数据所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data` | DataForSEO Trends data for the specified parameters | Trends time-series data points for the requested parameters. | 针对所请求参数的趋势时间序列数据点。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.date_from` | start date of the corresponding time range in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd” | Start date (UTC) of this data point's time bucket. | 该数据点所属时间桶的起始日期（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.date_to` | end date of the corresponding time range in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd” | End date (UTC) of this data point's time bucket. | 该数据点所属时间桶的结束日期（UTC）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.timestamp` | a point in time in the Unix time format | Point in time of this data point, in Unix time. | 该数据点的时间点，Unix 时间格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.data.values` | relative keyword popularity rate at a specific timestamp represents the keyword popularity rate over the given time range if you specify more than one keyword, the values will be averaged to the highest value across all specified keywords a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term. A value of 50 means that the term is half as popular. A score of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative keyword popularity at this timestamp; when multiple keywords are queried the values are averaged. The scale is relative, peaking at the most popular point. | 该时间点的相对关键词热度；查询多个关键词时取平均。该刻度为相对值，在最热点处达到峰值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.averages` | keyword popularity values averaged over the whole time range | Keyword popularity values averaged across the full requested time range. | 在整个所请求时间范围内取平均的关键词热度值。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_dataforseo_trends_locations

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | ![checked](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/wp-content/themes/dataforseo/assets/img/icons/checked-circle.svg) GET https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords\_data/dataforseo\_trends/locations | Return the reference list of DataForSEO Trends 位置 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 DataForSEO Trends 位置 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |
| `resp.200.country` | country ISO code optional field specify the ISO code if you want to filter the list of locations by country example: us | ISO country code to filter the returned list by; omit to list all entries. | 用于筛选返回列表的 ISO 国家代码；不传则列出全部条目。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_dataforseo_trends_subregion_interests_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with location-specific keyword popularity data from DataForSEO Trends. You can check keyword trends for Google Search, Google News, and Google Shopping. | Run a DataForSEO Trends 次区域兴趣 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 DataForSEO Trends 次区域兴趣 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field the maximum number of keywords you can specify: 5 avoid symbols and special characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis); specifying non-Latin characters, you’ll get data for the countries where they are used learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_name belongs to; example: United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you don’t use this field, you will recieve global results if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations note that the data will be provided for the country the specified location_code belongs to; example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.type` | dataforseo trends type optional field if you don’t specify this field, the web type will be used by default possible values: web, news, ecommerce | Trends data category to query (e.g. web, news, ecommerce). Selects which corpus the popularity figures are drawn from. | 要查询的趋势数据类别（如 web、news、ecommerce），决定热度数据取自哪一类语料。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the current day and month of the preceding year will be used by default minimal value for the web type: 2004-01-01 minimal value for other types: 2008-01-01 date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the today’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2019-01-15" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.time_range` | preset time ranges optional field if you specify date_from or date_to parameters, this field will be ignored when setting a task possible values for all type parameters: past_4_hours, past_day, past_7_days, past_30_days, past_90_days, past_12_months, past_5_years | Preset relative time window for trend data, used as a shortcut instead of date_from/date_to. Ignored if explicit dates are supplied. | 趋势数据的预设相对时间窗，作为 date_from/date_to 的快捷替代；若已显式给定日期则忽略本字段。 |
