| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.type` | type of element = ‘subregion_interests’ | Element type of this item row, indicating which kind of data block it carries. | 本条目的元素类型，指明它承载的数据块类别。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keywords` | relevant keywords the data included in the interests and interests_comparison is based on the keywords listed in this array | Keywords that the demography and comparison data in this item are based on. | 本条目中人口统计与对比数据所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests` | subregional keyword popuarity data for each specified term | Subregional keyword popularity data for each specified term. | 每个指定词的次区域关键词热度数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.keyword` | relevant keyword the data included in the values element is based on this keyword | Keyword the subregional values are based on. | 次区域数值所基于的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values` | contains data on relative keyword popularity by country or region | Relative keyword popularity broken down by country or region. | 按国家或地区拆分的相对关键词热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to the location parameters in your request. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求中的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to the location parameters in your request. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求中的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests.values.value` | relative keyword popularity rate in a given location represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using this value you can understand how popular a keyword is in one location compared to another location; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value for the relevant keyword across all locations, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the highest popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Location-specific relative keyword popularity over the requested time range. | 在所请求时间范围内某位置的相对关键词热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison` | comparison of data on subregional keyword popularity for the specified parameters if you specified a single keyword, the value will be null | Comparison of subregional popularity across the specified terms; null when only one keyword was supplied. | 对所指定多个词的次区域热度对比；仅提交一个关键词时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items` | keyword popularity values per location values in this array represent percentages relative to the maximum value within each region | Per-location popularity values normalized relative to the maximum within each region. | 按位置的热度值，相对每个地区内的最大值做归一化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.items.values` | keyword popularity rates within a given location represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using these values, you can understand which of the specified keywords is more popular in the related location; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value across all specified keywords within a given location, and then express the popularity values of each keyword as a percentage of the highest value (100); a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Relative popularity within the given location over the requested time range. | 在所请求时间范围内某位置内的相对热度。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items` | keyword popularity rates across all locations values in this array represent percentages relative to the maximum value across all locations | Per-location popularity values normalized relative to the maximum across all locations. | 按位置的热度值，相对所有位置中的最大值做归一化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.geo_id` | location identifier you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_id here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: US-NY | Location identifier; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置标识；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.geo_name` | location name you can use this field for matching obtained results with location parameters specified in the request see the full list of available locations with their geo_name here or by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/dataforseo_trends/locations example: Andorra | Location name; use it to match results back to your request's location parameters. | 位置名称；可用它把结果与请求的位置参数对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.interests_comparison.absolute_items.values` | keyword popularity rates relative to all locations represents location-specific keyword popularity rate over the specified time range; using these values, you can understand how popular each keyword is compared to all other keywords across all locations; the first value in the array is provided for the first term from the keywords array, the second value is provided for the second keyword, and so on; calculation: we determine the highest popularity value across all keywords across all locations, and then express all other values as a percentage of that highest value (100); a value of 100 is the peak popularity for the term a value of 50 means that the term is half as popular a value of 0 means there was not enough data for this term | Location-specific relative popularity, normalized across all locations. | 某位置的相对热度，跨所有位置做归一化。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_ad_traffic_by_keywords_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Google Ads 关键词流量预测 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Google Ads 关键词流量预测 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_ad_traffic_by_keywords_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Queue a Google Ads 关键词流量预测 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Google Ads 关键词流量预测 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 The maximum number of words for each keyword phrase: 10 the keywords you specify will be converted to a lowercase format Note #1: Google Ads may return no data for certain groups of keywords; Note #2: Google Ads provides combined search volume values for groups of similar keywords to obtain search volume for similar keywords, we recommend submitting such keywords in separate requests; Note #3: Google Ads doesn’t allow using certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis), so you can’t use them when setting a task; to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.bid` | the maximum custom bid required field the collected data will be based on this value it stands for the price you are willing to pay for an ad; the higher value you specify here, the higher values you will get in the returned metrics learn more in this help center article | Hypothetical max bid in USD used to forecast ad traffic. Drives the estimated impressions, clicks, and spend figures returned. | 用于预测广告流量的假设最高出价（美元），决定返回的预计展示、点击与花费数据。 |
| `req.match` | keywords match-type required field can take the following values: exact, broad, phrase | Keyword match type that controls how strictly user queries must match your keyword (aggregate / broad / phrase / exact), shaping which queries contribute to the metrics. | 关键词匹配类型，控制用户查询需与关键词匹配的严格程度（aggregate / broad / phrase / exact），影响哪些查询计入指标。 |
| `req.search_partners` | include Google search partners optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; default value: false – results are returned for Google search sites | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code; location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format; the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to; example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the forecasting time range required field if you specify date_to if you indicate date_from and date_to, you don’t need to specify date_interval minimum value is tomorrow’s date the value you specify in date_from shouldn’t be further than date_to date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2021-10-30"if Status endpoint returns false in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the month before last and prior; if Status endpoint returns true in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the last month and prior | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the forecasting time range required field if you specify date_from if you indicate date_from and date_to, you don’t need to specify date_interval minimum value is date_from +1 day maximum value is current day and month of the next year date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2022-10-30" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.date_interval` | forecasting date interval optional field if you specify date_interval, you don’t need to indicate date_from and date_to possible values: next_week, next_month, next_quarter default value: next_month | Forecasting horizon for ad-traffic estimates (e.g. next week/month/quarter), used as a shortcut instead of date_from/date_to. | 广告流量预测的预测区间（如下周/下月/下季度），作为 date_from/date_to 的快捷替代。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by relevance, impressions, ctr, average_cpc, cost, or clicks in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasksarray | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | unique task identifier in our system in the Universally unique identifier (UUID) format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_keywords_for_keywords_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Run a Google Ads 关键词扩展 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Google Ads 关键词扩展 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 20 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 the keywords you specify will be converted to a lowercase format Note: Google Ads may return no data for certain groups of keywords visit our Help Center to learn more Also note that Google Ads doesn’t allow using certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis), so you can’t use them when setting a task; to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. | `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code; location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format; the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to; example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. | `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.search_partners` | include Google search partners optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; default value: false – results are returned for Google search sites | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" minimal value: 4 years from the current date by default, data is returned for the past 12 months; Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than that specified in date_to and/or yesterday’s date;if Status endpoint returns false in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the month before last and prior; if Status endpoint returns true in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the last month and prior | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than yesterday’s date; if you don’t specify this field, yesterday’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2022-11-30" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by relevance, search_volume, competition_index, low_top_of_page_bid, or high_top_of_page_bid in descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.include_adult_keywords` | include keywords associated with adult content optional field if set to true, adult keywords will be included in the response default value: false note that the API may return no data for such keywords due to Google Ads restrictions | Whether adult-content keywords are kept in the response. Enable to retain them; note the provider may still return no data for such terms. | 是否在响应中保留成人内容关键词。开启则保留；注意此类词仍可能因提供方限制而无数据。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_keywords_for_keywords_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Google Ads 关键词扩展 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Google Ads 关键词扩展 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_keywords_for_keywords_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Queue a Google Ads 关键词扩展 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Google Ads 关键词扩展 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 20 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 the keywords you specify will be converted to a lowercase format Note: Google Ads may return no data for certain groups of keywords visit our Help Center to learn more Also note that Google Ads doesn’t allow using certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis), so you can’t use them when setting a task; to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.target` | target website optional field specify a website or URL to get a list of keywords relevant to it; Note: if a website url is specified, you will still get keywords relevant for the entire website | Target web page (or site) URL to scan for keyword ideas. Combine with target_type to choose page-level or site-level extraction. | 用于抓取关键词建议的目标网页（或站点）URL。与 target_type 搭配，决定按单页还是整站提取。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code; location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format; the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to; example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.search_partners` | include Google search partners optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; default value: false – results are returned for Google search sites | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" minimal value: 4 years from the current date by default, data is returned for the past 12 months; Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than that specified in date_to and/or yesterday’s date;if Status endpoint returns false in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the month before last and prior; if Status endpoint returns true in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the last month and prior | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than yesterday’s date; if you don’t specify this field, yesterday’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2022-11-30" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by relevance, search_volume, competition_index, low_top_of_page_bid, or high_top_of_page_bid in descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.include_adult_keywords` | include keywords associated with adult content optional field if set to true, adult keywords will be included in the response default value: false note that the API may return no data for such keywords due to Google Ads restrictions | Whether adult-content keywords are kept in the response. Enable to retain them; note the provider may still return no data for such terms. | 是否在响应中保留成人内容关键词。开启则保留；注意此类词仍可能因提供方限制而无数据。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Run a Google Ads 站点关键词 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Google Ads 站点关键词 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |

Use `site` to crawl the entire domain, `page` for the single URL in target. | 决定关键词建议是面向整站还是仅面向指定页面。`site` 抓取整个域名，`page` 仅针对 target 中的单个 URL。 |
