| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword` | keyword in a POST array | The keyword these metrics describe (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本组指标所对应的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_partners` | include Google search partners the value you specified when setting the task if true, the results are returned for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; if false, the results are returned for Google search sites only | Whether partner-network data was included in this result. | 本结果是否纳入了合作网络的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition` | competition represents the relative level of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only possible values: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH if competition level is unknown, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Relative paid-search competition level for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词在付费搜索中的相对竞争程度；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition_index` | competition index the competition index for the query indicating how competitive ad placement is for the keyword can take values from 0 to 100 the level of competition from 0 to 100 is determined by the number of ad slots filled divided by the total number of ad slots available if not enough data is available, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Competition score reflecting how contested ad placement is for the keyword (higher means more competitive); null when data is insufficient. | 反映该关键词广告位竞争激烈程度的竞争指数（越高越激烈）；数据不足时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea either on google.com or google.com and partners, depending on the user’s targeting if there is no data, the value is null | Approximate monthly average number of searches for the keyword under the requested targeting. | 在所请求定向下，该关键词的月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Lower-end estimated bid (USD) needed to show at the top of the first results page; varies with the requested location. | 在首页顶部展示所需出价的下限估值（美元），随所请求位置而变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Upper-end estimated bid (USD) needed to show at the top of the first results page; varies with the requested location. | 在首页顶部展示所需出价的上限估值（美元），随所请求位置而变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.cpc` | cost per click indicates the amount paid (USD) for each click on the ad displayed for a given keyword | Average historical cost-per-click in USD for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词的历史平均每次点击成本（美元）；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations if there is no data, the value is null | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword over the trailing window. | 该关键词在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword_annotations` | the annotations for the keyword | Annotation details attached to the keyword. | 附加在该关键词上的注解信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.concepts` | the list of concepts for the keyword | Concepts associated with the keyword, grouping it into broader themes. | 与关键词关联的概念，将其归入更宏观的主题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.concepts.name` | the concept name for the keyword in the concept_group | Concept name for the keyword within its concept group. | 关键词在其概念组内的概念名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.concepts.concept_group` | the concept group of the concept details | The concept group this concept belongs to. | 该概念所属的概念组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.concepts.concept_group.name` | the concept group name | Name of the concept group. | 概念组的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.concepts.concept_group.type` | the concept group type | Type of the concept group. | 概念组的类型。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_keywords_for_site_task_get_id

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Google Ads 站点关键词 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Google Ads 站点关键词 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_keywords_for_site_task_post

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Queue a Google Ads 站点关键词 task for asynchronous processing; the response returns a task id you later fetch via the matching task_get endpoint. Optionally set postback_url/pingback_url to be notified on completion. | 提交一个 Google Ads 站点关键词 任务异步处理；响应返回任务 id，稍后通过对应的 task_get 端点取回结果。可选地设置 postback_url/pingback_url 以在完成时获得通知。 |
| `req.target` | domain or page required field the domain name of the target website or the url of the target page; note: to obtain keywords for the target website, use the target_type parameter | Target web page (or site) URL to scan for keyword ideas. Combine with target_type to choose page-level or site-level extraction. | 用于抓取关键词建议的目标网页（或站点）URL。与 target_type 搭配，决定按单页还是整站提取。 |
| `req.target_type` | search keywords for site or url optional field possible values: site, page; default value: page if set to site, keywords will be provided for the entire site; if set to page, keywords will be provided for the specified webpage | Whether keyword ideas are derived for the whole site or only the given page. Use `site` to crawl the entire domain, `page` for the single URL in target. | 决定关键词建议是面向整站还是仅面向指定页面。`site` 抓取整个域名，`page` 仅针对 target 中的单个 URL。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code; location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format; the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to; example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.search_partners` | include Google search partners optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; default value: false – results are returned for Google search sites | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" minimal value: 4 years from the current date by default, data is returned for the past 12 months; Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than that specified in date_to and/or yesterday’s date;if Status endpoint returns false in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the month before last and prior; if Status endpoint returns true in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the last month and prior | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than yesterday’s date; if you don’t specify this field, yesterday’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2022-11-30" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.include_adult_keywords` | include keywords associated with adult content optional field if set to true, adult keywords will be included in the response default value: false note that the API may return no data for such keywords due to Google Ads restrictions | Whether adult-content keywords are kept in the response. Enable to retain them; note the provider may still return no data for such terms. | 是否在响应中保留成人内容关键词。开启则保留；注意此类词仍可能因提供方限制而无数据。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field Use these parameters to sort the results by relevance, search_volume, competition_index, low_top_of_page_bid, or high_top_of_page_bid in descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.postback_url` | URL for sending task results optional field once the task is completed, we will send a POST request with its results compressed in the gzip format to the postback_url you specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request. example: http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/postbackscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in postback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a POST callback with the gzipped task results once the task finishes. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, which are substituted before the callback is sent. | 任务完成后接收回调的地址，结果以 gzip 压缩通过 POST 推送到此。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.pingback_url` | notification URL of a completed task optional field when a task is completed we will notify you by GET request sent to the URL you have specified you can use the ‘$id’ string as a $id variable and ‘$tag’ as urlencoded $tag variable. We will set the necessary values before sending the request example: http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id http://your-server.com/pingscript?id=$id&tag=$tag Note: special characters in pingback_url will be urlencoded; i.a., the # character will be encoded into %23 learn more on our Help Center | Endpoint that receives a lightweight GET ping when the task completes, signalling you to fetch the results. Supports the `$id` and `$tag` placeholders, substituted before the ping is sent. | 任务完成时接收 GET 通知的地址，用于提示你去拉取结果。支持 `$id`、`$tag` 占位符，发送前会被替换为实际值。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results in this case, the value will be null | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |

## post_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_search_volume_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Run a Google Ads 搜索量 request synchronously and get the data back in the same response, with no separate task to poll. | 以同步方式发起 Google Ads 搜索量 请求，在同一响应中直接拿到数据，无需另行轮询任务。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 1000 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 The maximum number of words for each keyword phrase: 10 the keywords you specify will be converted to a lowercase format Note #1: Google Ads may return no data for certain groups of keywords; Note #2: Google Ads provides combined search volume values for groups of similar keywords to obtain search volume for similar keywords, we recommend submitting such keywords in separate requests; Note #3: Google Ads doesn’t allow using certain symbols and characters (e.g., UTF symbols, emojis), so you can’t use them when setting a task; to learn more about which symbols and characters can be used, please refer to this article learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Seed keywords to analyze; pass them as an array of strings. Capping and character rules are enforced by the endpoint, and non-Latin characters bias results toward the regions where those characters are used. | 待分析的种子关键词，以字符串数组传入。条数上限与字符规则由端点强制；使用非拉丁字符会让结果偏向这些字符所属的地区。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of search engine location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code or location_coordinate you can receive the list of available locations of the search engine with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: London,England,United Kingdom | Full location name used for geo targeting (e.g. country, region, city). Mutually replaceable with location_code; omit both to get global results. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages / locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的位置全名（如国家、地区、城市）。与 location_code 二选一；两者都不传则返回全球结果。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages / locations 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | search engine location code optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_coordinate; you can receive the list of available locations of the search engines with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/locations example: 2840 | Numeric location identifier used for geo targeting; an alternative to location_name. Omit both to get global results. Data is reported for the country the code belongs to. Look up valid codes via the matching locations endpoint. | 用于地理定向的数字位置标识，可替代 location_name。两者都不传则返回全球结果；数据按该编码所属国家提供。可通过对应的 locations 端点查询合法编码。 |
| `req.location_coordinate` | GPS coordinates of a location optional field if you do not indicate the location, you will receive worldwide results, i.e., for all available locations; if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name or location_code; location_coordinate parameter should be specified in the “latitude,longitude” format; the data will be provided for the country the specified coordinates belong to; example: 52.6178549,-155.352142 | GPS-based geo target given as `latitude,longitude,radius_km`. An alternative to location_name / location_code; data is reported for the country the coordinates fall in. | 基于 GPS 的地理定向，格式为 `纬度,经度,半径(km)`。可替代 location_name / location_code；数据按坐标所属国家提供。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of search engine language optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: English | Full search-engine language name (e.g. English) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_code. Look up valid names via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言全名（如 English），与 language_code 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | search engine language code optional field you can receive the list of available languages of the search engine with their language_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/languages example: en | Search-engine language code (e.g. en) for the query. Mutually replaceable with language_name. Look up valid codes via the matching locations_and_languages endpoint. | 查询使用的搜索引擎语言代码（如 en），与 language_name 二选一。可通过对应的 locations_and_languages 端点查询合法代码。 |
| `req.search_partners` | include Google search partners optional field if you specify true, the results will be delivered for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; default value: false – results are returned for Google search sites | Whether to include syndicated search-partner networks in addition to the primary engine. Enable to widen reach across partner sites. | 是否在主引擎之外纳入联合搜索合作网络。开启可把覆盖范围扩展到合作站点。 |
| `req.date_from` | starting date of the time range optional field date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" minimal value: 4 years from the current date by default, data is returned for the past 12 months; Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than that specified in date_to and/or yesterday’s date;if Status endpoint returns false in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the month before last and prior; if Status endpoint returns true in the actual_data field, date_from can be set to the last month and prior | Start of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Endpoint-specific minimum dates apply; omit to default to the start of the comparable prior period. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的起始日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。各端点有各自的最早可用日期；不传时按可比的上一周期起点默认。 |
| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field Note: the indicated date cannot be greater than the past month, Google Ads does not return data on the current month; if you don’t specify this field, yesterday’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2022-11-30" | End of the time window for historical/trend data, in `yyyy-mm-dd`. Omit to default to the current date. | 历史/趋势数据时间窗的结束日期，格式 `yyyy-mm-dd`。不传则默认到当天。 |
| `req.include_adult_keywords` | include keywords associated with adult content optional field if set to true, adult keywords will be included in the response default value: false note that the API may return no data for such keywords due to Google Ads restrictions | Whether adult-content keywords are kept in the response. Enable to retain them; note the provider may still return no data for such terms. | 是否在响应中保留成人内容关键词。开启则保留；注意此类词仍可能因提供方限制而无数据。 |
| `req.sort_by` | results sorting parameters optional field use these parameters to sort the results by relevance, search_volume, competition_index, low_top_of_page_bid, or high_top_of_page_bid in the descending order default value: relevance | Metric used to order the returned keyword rows in descending order (e.g. by search volume, CPC, competition, or relevance). | 返回关键词行的降序排序依据（如按搜索量、CPC、竞争度或相关度）。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data array of the response | Your own label for the task, echoed back in the response so you can correlate results with the request that produced them. | 自定义的任务标签，会原样回显在响应中，方便把结果与触发它的请求对应起来。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version string that produced this response; useful when reporting issues. | 生成本响应的 API 版本号，反馈问题时可一并提供。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall response status code for the request; check it before reading the payload and design handling for error conditions. | 本次请求的总体状态码；读取数据前应先检查，并为异常情况设计处理逻辑。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message accompanying the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明文字。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Server-side processing time for the request, in seconds. | 本次请求的服务端处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total billed cost of this response across all tasks, in USD. | 本响应所有任务的合计计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task entries contained in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中包含的任务条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | How many of the tasks finished with an error; if non-zero, inspect each task's own status fields. | 其中以错误结束的任务数量；若不为 0，需逐个检查任务自身的状态字段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task results; one entry per task created by the request. | 任务结果列表，请求创建的每个任务对应一个条目。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique identifier (UUID) of this task in the provider's system. | 该任务在提供方系统中的唯一标识（UUID）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message for this task's status code. | 该任务状态码对应的可读说明。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Processing time for this individual task, in seconds. | 单个任务的处理耗时，单位秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Billed cost of this individual task, in USD. | 单个任务的计费金额，单位美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of entries in this task's result array. | 该任务 result 数组中的条目数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.keyword` | keyword keyword is returned with decoded %## (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) | The keyword these metrics describe (URL-decoded; `+` becomes a space). | 本组指标所对应的关键词（已 URL 解码，`+` 还原为空格）。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.spell` | correct spelling of the keyword Note:if the keyword in the POST array appears to be misspelled, data will be returned for the correctly spelled keyword; we use the functionality of Google Ads API to check and validate the spelling of keywords, learn more by this link | Corrected spelling of the submitted keyword; when the input looks misspelled, data is returned for this corrected term. | 提交关键词的纠正拼写；当输入疑似拼错时，会返回纠正后词条的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的位置编码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data is available. | 从请求回显的语言代码；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_partners` | indicates whether data from partner networks included in the response | Whether partner-network data was included in this result. | 本结果是否纳入了合作网络的数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; this value is based on Google Ads data and can take the following values: HIGH, MEDIUM, LOW; if there is no data the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Relative paid-search competition level for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词在付费搜索中的相对竞争程度；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.competition_index` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; this value is based on Google Ads data and can be between 0 and 100 (inclusive); if there is no data the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Competition score reflecting how contested ad placement is for the keyword (higher means more competitive); null when data is insufficient. | 反映该关键词广告位竞争激烈程度的竞争指数（越高越激烈）；数据不足时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate; represents either the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea on google.com or google.com and partners, depending on the user’s targeting; if there is no data then the value is null | Approximate monthly average number of searches for the keyword under the requested targeting. | 在所请求定向下，该关键词的月均搜索量近似值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers); the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Lower-end estimated bid (USD) needed to show at the top of the first results page; varies with the requested location. | 在首页顶部展示所需出价的下限估值（美元），随所请求位置而变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers); the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Upper-end estimated bid (USD) needed to show at the top of the first results page; varies with the requested location. | 在首页顶部展示所需出价的上限估值（美元），随所请求位置而变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.cpc` | cost per click indicates the amount paid (USD) for each click on the ad displayed for a given keyword | Average historical cost-per-click in USD for the keyword; null when no data is available. | 该关键词的历史平均每次点击成本（美元）；无数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months by default), targeted to the specified geographic locations; if there is no data then the value is null | Per-month search-volume history for the keyword over the trailing window. | 该关键词在最近窗口内逐月的搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.year` | year | Year of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.month` | month | Month of this monthly data point. | 该月度数据点所属月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate | Average search volume for that month. | 该月份的平均搜索量。 |

| `(operation)` | Note that Google Ads Keywords Data API is based on the latest version of the [Google Ads API](https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/docs/start) that has replaced legacy Google AdWords API. If you’re using [DataForSEO Google AdWords API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google/overview.md), you need to upgrade to [DataForSEO Google Ads API](https://docs.dataforseo.com/v3/keywords_data/google_ads/overview.md). | Retrieve the results of a previously queued Google Ads 搜索量 task by its task id. | 按任务 id 取回此前排队的 Google Ads 搜索量 任务结果。 |
| `resp.200.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format you will be able to use it within 30 days to request the results of the task at any time | Unique task identifier (UUID) you can use to retrieve this task's results later from the corresponding task_get endpoint. | 任务的唯一标识（UUID），后续可凭它从对应的 task_get 端点取回该任务结果。 |

## get_dataforseo_keywords_data_google_ads_status

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | By calling this endpoint, you will know if Google updated keyword data for the previous month. Generally, Google updates keyword data in the middle of the month. So, if Google updated its data in October, you would be able to see the actual search volume, cost-per-click, competition, and other metrics for September. If Google didn’t update its data in October, the latest information would be available for August. | Return the reference list of Google Ads 状态 supported by the Keywords Data API, used to fill targeting parameters in other endpoints. | 返回 Keywords Data API 支持的 Google Ads 状态 参考列表，用于填写其它端点的定向参数。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of response codes here | Per-task status code; check it to tell whether this individual task succeeded. | 单个任务的状态码，用于判断该任务是否成功。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments identifying the endpoint that handled this task. | 标识处理该任务的端点的 URL 路径片段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | the data specified in the API call | Echo of the parameters you submitted in the request, returned for traceability. | 回显你在请求中提交的参数，便于追溯。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Array carrying the actual keyword/trend data produced for this task; drill into its items for per-keyword figures. | 承载该任务实际关键词/趋势数据的数组，逐项下钻可得到按关键词的具体数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.actual_data` | indicates whether Google updated keyword data for the previous month generally, Google updates keyword data in the middle of the month if the value is true, Google currently provides up-to-date data for the previous month if the value is false, we are not able to provide data for the previous month | Whether up-to-date keyword data for the previous month is available; false means last month's data could not be provided. | 是否已有上个月的最新关键词数据；false 表示无法提供上月数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.date_update` | date of the latest update of Google Ads data indicates the latest date when Google updated search volume, CPC, and other keyword metrics example: 2020-05-15 | Date of the latest provider-side refresh of the underlying keyword metrics. | 底层关键词指标在提供方侧最近一次更新的日期。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.last_year_in_monthly_searches` | the latest year for which search volume data is available | Most recent year for which monthly search-volume data is available. | 月度搜索量数据可用的最近年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.last_month_in_monthly_searches` | the latest month for which search volume data is available | Most recent month for which monthly search-volume data is available. | 月度搜索量数据可用的最近月份。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.category_code_parent` | the code of the superordinate category example: "category_code": 1100, "category_name": "Superhero Films", "category_code_parent": 1097 where category_code_parent corresponds to: "category_code": 1097, "category_name": "Action & Adventure Films" | Category code of the parent (superordinate) Google Trends category. | 上级（父级）Google Trends 类目的类目编码。 |
